/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPINT_BILLING_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPINT_BILLING_PRC]
AS
BEGIN

SET NOCOUNT ON;

DECLARE
@p1 VARCHAR(100),@p2 VARCHAR(100),@p3 VARCHAR(100),@p4 VARCHAR(100),@p5 VARCHAR(100),@p6 VARCHAR(100),
@p7 VARCHAR(100),@p8 VARCHAR(100),@p9 VARCHAR(100),@p10 VARCHAR(100),@p11 VARCHAR(100),@p12 VARCHAR(100);

DECLARE VP_CURSOR CURSOR FOR 
SELECT 
commercial_project_id, --1,
item_number_of_the_SD_document,--2
'dummy_sequence' dummy_seq, --3,
'dummy_billing_date' dummy_billing_date, --4,
CASE WHEN sales_document_item_category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1
     WHEN sales_document_item_category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN
            CASE WHEN charge_per IN ('Two Months') THEN ROUND(total_fee/2,2)
            WHEN charge_per IN ('Four Months') THEN ROUND(total_fee/4,2)
	        WHEN charge_per IN ('Semi-Annually') THEN ROUND(total_fee/6,2)
	        ELSE total_fee
            END
END AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,--5
CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE) Service_Start_Date_ETL,--6
--DATEADD(YEAR,1,CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE)) Service_Start_Date_ETL,
CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN charge_per = 'One Off' THEN todate  ELSE end_date_wp_etl END,1,10) AS DATE) Service_End_Date_ETL,--7
material_number,--8
wp_description,--9
sales_document_item_category,--10
src,--11,
charge_per --12
--start_date_wp_etl,fromdate,todate,charge_per,total_fee
FROM 
dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;
--WHERE CHARGE_PER='Monthly' and commercial_project_id = 'M110000507' AND Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document='3';

TRUNCATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING];

OPEN VP_CURSOR;

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;

WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN

	IF @P12 IN ('One Off')
	BEGIN
	      INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
		  SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',@P6,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;
	END

   ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Annually')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',START_DT,@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END 
	ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Quarterly')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END

   ELSE --Monthly, 2 Months, 4 Months, semi-Annually
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_BILLING]
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);

	END

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12;

END

CLOSE VP_CURSOR;
DEALLOCATE VP_CURSOR;

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE              PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_PRC] 
AS

BEGIN

--TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE;

--INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE
SELECT CCTR.Cost_Center_ctr,
A.*
INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE
FROM
(
SELECT 
COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,Work_Package_Name_ETL) work_package_dup,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE ORDER BY Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Sequence_Number,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE ORDER BY Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document--,
,a.*
FROM (
SELECT DISTINCT 
        SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,10) AS New_Service_Start_Date,
		SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_End_Date,1,10) AS New_Service_End_Date,
		SUBSTRING(vp.New_Billing_Date,1,10) AS New_Billing_Date,
		vp.Frequency,
		vp.New_Billing_Amount,
        vp.src,
	   'M2'+vp.Master_File_Code AS Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,
        vp.Master_File_Code,
		vp.send_invoice_to,
		vp.Invoice_Billing_File,
		--vp.projects,
		CASE WHEN vp.NEW_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U' ELSE NULL END AS WP_Type,
		CASE WHEN vp.NEW_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U003' ELSE NULL END AS Service_ID,
		CASE WHEN vp.NEW_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN '1' ELSE NULL END AS Service_Quantity,
		CONVERT(VARCHAR,
		MIN(CAST(SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,10) AS DATE)) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code)
		,104) AS Start_Date,
	    CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,10) AS DATE),104) AS Start_Date_wp,
		SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,10) AS Start_Date_wp_ETL,
	    CASE WHEN LEFT(New_Work_Package_Name,58) IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE LEFT(New_Work_Package_Name,58) END AS Work_Package_Name_ETL,
		CASE WHEN xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW IS NULL OR xref3.CUSTOMER_NEW IS NULL THEN 'NO'
		     WHEN vp.Master_File_Code <> vp.send_invoice_to OR 
		 (vp.Master_File_Code <> vp.Invoice_Billing_File AND vp.Invoice_Billing_File IS NOT NULL) OR
		 (vp.send_invoice_to <> vp.Invoice_Billing_File AND  vp.Invoice_Billing_File IS NOT NULL)
		THEN  'YES' ELSE 'NO' END SO_Header_Partner_flag,
		--CASE WHEN vp.Master_File_Code = vp.projects THEN xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW 
		--     WHEN vp.Master_File_Code = vp.send_invoice_to THEN xref.CUSTOMER_NEW 
		--END AS Customer,
		CASE WHEN vp.Invoice_Billing_File IS NOT NULL AND vp.Invoice_Billing_File <> vp.Send_Invoice_to AND 
		          vp.Invoice_Billing_File <> vp.Master_File_Code 
				  THEN xref3.CUSTOMER_NEW
		     ELSE xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW
		END AS Customer,
	   'M2'+vp.New_product AS Material_Number,
	   vp.NEW_Item_Category AS Sales_Document_Item_Category,
	   xref.CUSTOMER_NEW AS Customer_ID,
       --COALESCE(xref.CUSTOMER_NEW,vp.Master_File_Code)  AS Customer_ID,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,YEAR(CAST(SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,10) AS DATE))) Calendar_Year,
	   RIGHT('0'+MONTH(CAST(SUBSTRING(vp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,10) AS DATE)),2) Calendar_Month,
       vp.RelationShip_Manager_Name,
	   vp.Senior_RelationShip_Manager_Name,
	   vp.File_Handler_Name,
       CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN 'VFS'
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN 'VGS'
			ELSE 'OTHERS'
			END segment_name_original,
       CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN 'VFS'
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN 'VGS'
			ELSE 'VFS'
			END segment_name,
       CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN '50100000' 
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN '80100000'  
			ELSE '50100000'
	   END AS Profit_Center,
  	  CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN '50100000'
	      WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN COALESCE(PCTR.PROFIT_center_code,'80100000')
		  ELSE '50100000'
	  END AS Profit_Center_item,
	   Master_File_Name AS Project_Name,
	   'C' AS Project_Type,
	   'P003' AS Stage,
		'31.12.2040' AS End_Date,
		'31.12.2030' AS End_Date_wp,
		'2030-12-31' AS End_Date_wp_ETL,
		Currency AS Currency,
		RevEntity AS Service_Organization,
		RevEntity AS Company_Code,
	   'N'                 AS Indicator__Restr__Time_Post__W_O_Staff_,
       'X'                 AS Project_Invoicing_Solution,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(SUM(CAST(vp.New_Billing_Amount AS FLOAT)) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code),2))  ACV_Value,
	   LEFT(RevEntity,2) AS CDM,
	   'NA' AS Closure_Reason,
	   '01.01.2026' AS First_Price_Refresh_Date,
	   '0' AS PI_______Number,
       'Yes' AS Price_Increase_PI____Indicator,
	   '0SAP_RL_005' AS Project_Role_ID,
	   CASE WHEN vp.New_Work_Package_Description IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE New_Work_Package_Description END AS WP_Description,
	   'RE' AS Partner_Function,
	   CASE WHEN vp.New_Work_Package_Name IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE vp.New_Work_Package_Name END AS Material_Description,
		vp.Service_Country AS Price_Refresh___Country,
		CAST(vp.New_Billing_Amount AS FLOAT) Total_Fee
FROM 
(
SELECT
VP.*
FROM 
(
SELECT   'ORIGINAL' SRC,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V]
 UNION ALL 
 SELECT  'DRE' SRC,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_DRE_V] 
 UNION ALL
 SELECT  'BUDDY' SRC,* FROM DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_BUDDY_V 
)vp
) vp
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref
ON vp.Master_File_Code = xref.CUSTOMER_OLD 
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref2
ON vp.Send_Invoice_to = xref2.CUSTOMER_OLD 
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref3
ON vp.Invoice_Billing_File = xref3.CUSTOMER_OLD 
LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_SEGMENT] CTR
ON CTR.Company_Code = VP.RevEntity AND
CTR.Customer = vp.Master_File_Code
LEFT OUTER JOIN  SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROFIT_CTR_ITEM_V PCTR
ON PCTR.LEGACY_PRODUCT = VP.New_product
)A
)A
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_COST_CTR cctr
ON CHARINDEX(a.segment_name, cctr.segment_ctr) > 0 AND
   CHARINDEX(a.Company_Code, cctr.Company_Code_ctr) > 0
WHERE Cost_Center_ctr IS NOT NULL AND Customer_ID IS NOT NULL 
AND FREQUENCY IN ('One Time','Monthly','Quarterly','Semi Annual','Annual');

PRINT 'XREF FOR COMMERICAL PROJECT ID';
INSERT INTO Commercial_Project_ID_XREF
SELECT f.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,
'C'+CAST(NEXT VALUE FOR Commercial_Project_ID_Seq AS NVARCHAR(1000)) AS Commercial_Project_ID,
'VP' SRC
FROM
(SELECT DISTINCT Commercial_Project_ID_PRE FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE) f
LEFT OUTER JOIN Commercial_Project_ID_XREF xref
ON xref.Commercial_Project_ID_Pre = f.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE
WHERE xref.Commercial_Project_ID IS NULL;

PRINT 'INSERT FINAL';
--TRUNCATE TABLE  DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;

--INSERT INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG
SELECT 
XREF.Commercial_Project_ID AS Commercial_Project_ID,
XREF.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE AS Commercial_Project_ID_PRE_XREF,
F.*
INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG
FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE F
LEFT OUTER JOIN Commercial_Project_ID_XREF XREF
ON F.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE = XREF.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE;

END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_PRC_BKP]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create          PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_PRC_BKP] 
AS

BEGIN

TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE;
--drop table dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE;

INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE
SELECT 
COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,Work_Package_Name_ETL) work_package_dup,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE ORDER BY Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Sequence_Number,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE ORDER BY Work_Package_Name_ETL,material_number)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document--,
--CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE ORDER BY Billing_Due_Date)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_for_Billing_Plan_Invoice_Plan_Paym,
,a.*
--INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE
FROM (
SELECT DISTINCT 
       vp.src,
	   'M2.1'+vp.Master_File_Code AS Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,
        vp.Master_File_Code,
		vp.send_invoice_to,
		vp.Invoice_Billing_File,
		--vp.projects,
		CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U' ELSE NULL END AS WP_Type,
		CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U003' ELSE NULL END AS Service_ID,
		CASE WHEN vp.item_category IN ('PS07') THEN '1' ELSE NULL END AS Service_Quantity,
		CONVERT(VARCHAR,
		MIN(CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE)) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code)
		,104) AS Start_Date,
	    CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE),104) AS Start_Date_wp,
		FromDate AS Start_Date_wp_ETL,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(SUBSTRING(NextDate,1,10) AS DATE),104) AS Billing_Due_Date,
	    CASE WHEN LEFT(Rdescription,58) IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE LEFT(Rdescription,58) END AS Work_Package_Name_ETL,
		CASE WHEN xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW IS NULL OR xref3.CUSTOMER_NEW IS NULL THEN 'NO'
		     WHEN vp.Master_File_Code <> vp.send_invoice_to OR 
		 (vp.Master_File_Code <> vp.Invoice_Billing_File AND vp.Invoice_Billing_File IS NOT NULL) OR
		 (vp.send_invoice_to <> vp.Invoice_Billing_File AND  vp.Invoice_Billing_File IS NOT NULL)
		THEN  'YES' ELSE 'NO' END SO_Header_Partner_flag,
		--CASE WHEN vp.Master_File_Code = vp.projects THEN xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW 
		--     WHEN vp.Master_File_Code = vp.send_invoice_to THEN xref.CUSTOMER_NEW 
		--END AS Customer,
		CASE WHEN vp.Invoice_Billing_File IS NOT NULL AND vp.Invoice_Billing_File <> vp.Send_Invoice_to AND 
		          vp.Invoice_Billing_File <> vp.Master_File_Code 
				  THEN xref3.CUSTOMER_NEW
		     ELSE xref2.CUSTOMER_NEW
		END AS Customer,
	   'M2.1'+vp.New_S4_product AS Material_Number,
	   vp.item_category AS Sales_Document_Item_Category,
	   xref.CUSTOMER_NEW AS Customer_ID,
       --COALESCE(xref.CUSTOMER_NEW,vp.Master_File_Code)  AS Customer_ID,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,YEAR(CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE))) Calendar_Year,
	   RIGHT('0'+MONTH(CAST(SUBSTRING(FromDate,1,10) AS DATE)),2) Calendar_Month,
       vp.RelationShip_Manager_Name,
	   vp.Senior_RelationShip_Manager_Name,
	   vp.File_Handler_Name,
       RevEntity+'901110' AS Cost_Center_ETL, --LKP (RevEntity]) Need Lookup
 	   '90100000' AS Profit_Center_ETL, --LKP ,Need Lookup (RevEntity,Cost Centre) , Many center there for the same RevEntity/Comp_code
	   Master_File_Name AS Project_Name,
	   'C' AS Project_Type,
	   'P003' AS Stage,
		'31.12.2040' AS End_Date,
		'31.12.2029' AS End_Date_wp,
		'2029-12-31' AS End_Date_wp_ETL,
		Matter_Currency AS Currency,
		RevEntity AS Service_Organization,
		RevEntity AS Company_Code,
	   'N'                 AS Indicator__Restr__Time_Post__W_O_Staff_,
       'X'                 AS Project_Invoicing_Solution,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(SUM(CAST(Total_Fee AS FLOAT)) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code),2))  ACV_Value,
	   LEFT(RevEntity,2) AS CDM,
	   'NA' AS Closure_Reason,
	   '01.01.2026' AS First_Price_Refresh_Date,
	   '0' AS PI_______Number,
       'Yes' AS Price_Increase_PI____Indicator,
	   '0SAP_RL_005' AS Project_Role_ID,
	   CASE WHEN Rdescription IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE Rdescription END AS WP_Description,
	   'RE' AS Partner_Function,
	   CASE WHEN Rdescription IS NULL THEN Master_File_Code ELSE Rdescription END AS Material_Description,
		vp.Service_Country AS Price_Refresh___Country,
        vp.EffectDate,
		vp.NextDate,
       --to handle data quality issue with oneoff frequency where fromdate is larger than todate, the below fix has implemented
		CASE WHEN CAST(SUBSTRING(FROMDATE,1,10) AS DATE) > CAST(SUBSTRING(TODATE,1,10) AS DATE) THEN vp.ToDate ELSE vp.FromDate END FromDate,
		CASE WHEN CAST(SUBSTRING(FROMDATE,1,10) AS DATE) > CAST(SUBSTRING(TODATE,1,10) AS DATE) THEN vp.FromDate ELSE vp.ToDate END ToDate,
		CAST(Total_Fee AS FLOAT) Total_Fee,
		Charge_Per
FROM 
(
SELECT
--SUM(CASE WHEN vp.item_category='PS06' THEN CAST(Total_Fee AS FLOAT) ELSE 0 END) OVER (PARTITION BY Master_File_Code) AS Total_Fee_ETL,
VP.*
FROM 
(
SELECT   'ORIGINAL' SRC,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_EXTRACT_FILTER_V]
 UNION ALL 
 SELECT  'DRE' SRC,* FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_DRE_DUMMY_V] 
 UNION ALL
 SELECT  'BUDDY' SRC,* FROM DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VP_BUDDY_V 
)vp
) vp
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref
ON vp.Master_File_Code = xref.CUSTOMER_OLD 
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref2
ON vp.Send_Invoice_to = xref2.CUSTOMER_OLD 
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF xref3
ON vp.Invoice_Billing_File = xref3.CUSTOMER_OLD 
)A;
--WHERE Customer_ID IS NOT NULL;

PRINT 'XREF FOR COMMERICAL PROJECT ID';
INSERT INTO Commercial_Project_ID_XREF
SELECT f.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,
'C'+CAST(NEXT VALUE FOR Commercial_Project_ID_Seq AS NVARCHAR(1000)) AS Commercial_Project_ID,
'VP' SRC
FROM
(SELECT DISTINCT Commercial_Project_ID_PRE FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE) f
LEFT OUTER JOIN Commercial_Project_ID_XREF xref
ON xref.Commercial_Project_ID_Pre = f.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE
WHERE xref.Commercial_Project_ID IS NULL;

PRINT 'INSERT FINAL';
TRUNCATE TABLE  DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;
--DROP TABLE DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG;

INSERT INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG
SELECT 
XREF.Commercial_Project_ID AS Commercial_Project_ID,
XREF.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE AS Commercial_Project_ID_PRE_XREF,
F.*
--INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG
FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_VIEWPOINT_STG_PRE F
LEFT OUTER JOIN Commercial_Project_ID_XREF XREF
ON F.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE = XREF.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE;

END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE         PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP] 
AS
BEGIN


EXEC [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC];
PRINT 'Complete Freq_prc';

TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2;
--TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER;

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0';
WITH WP AS
(
SELECT 
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old 
                        ORDER BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,bill_to_key,currency_key,Execution_Country_key,category_key
          			    )  AS VARCHAR(100))  new_project_number,
w.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       wp.[Project_Definition]  AS Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       wp.Work_Package_WBS, 
	   wp.[Work_Package_WBS_Desc],
	   COALESCE(bill_to,'0') AS bill_to_key,
	   COALESCE(currency,'0') AS currency_key,
       CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL THEN 'G1' 
	        WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NOT NULL THEN wp.Execution_Country
			WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NULL THEN LEFT(wp.Company_Code,2) 
			END AS Execution_Country_Key,
	   COALESCE(a.category,'0') category_key,
	   UPPER(COALESCE(product, '0')) as product_key, 
	   CASE WHEN a.product_advisory IS NOT NULL THEN '1' ELSE '0' END AS advisory_flag_key,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='LEGAL' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END legal_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='TAX'   THEN '1' ELSE 0 END tax_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='HR'    THEN '1' ELSE 0 END hr_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN CHARINDEX('DRE', UPPER(COALESCE(product_1, '0')))>0 THEN '1' ELSE 0 END dre_exists_flag,
	   --CASE WHEN b.action = 'FILTER' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END prd_filter_flag
	   '0' prd_filter_flag
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
INNER JOIN SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ F
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = f.plan_item_vf AND
   wp.[Project_Definition] = f.[Project_Definition_vf]
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_ADVISORY A
ON wp.PRODUCT = A.PRODUCT_ADVISORY
--LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.sap_in_project_product_bridge b
--ON wp.PRODUCT = B.PRODUCT_OLD
) w
),
WP1 AS
(
SELECT 'M2'+Commericial_Project_id_Old+'A'+new_project_number AS Commericial_Project_id_new, WP.*,
MAX(dre_exists_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS dre_exists_group_flag,
MAX(prd_filter_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS prd_filter_group_flag
FROM WP 
),
WP2 AS
(--Everything
SELECT * FROM WP1 --WHERE prd_filter_group_flag <> 1
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
SELECT * FROM WP2;

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1';
WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
SELECT * FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY 
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2';
WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
), 
WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,'ORIGINAL' SRC 
FROM
WP2 x WHERE x.Work_Package_WBS NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT y.Work_Package_WBS 
                                        FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY y
										WHERE y.src NOT LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
									  )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
SELECT * FROM WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER';
WITH ALL_DATA AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
UNION 
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER 
SELECT z.*,CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_old ORDER BY work_package_wbs)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_etl_join,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_new ORDER BY work_package_wbs,src)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_group_etl_join,
CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), GETDATE(), 120) AS ENTRY_DATE,
'Y' Active_flag
FROM ALL_DATA z
WHERE Z.Commericial_Project_id_Old NOT IN (SELECT i.Commericial_Project_id_Old FROM dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER i)
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'UPDATE PROJECT FILTER';
UPDATE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER 
SET ACTIVE_FLAG = 'N - FILTER'
WHERE commericial_project_id_new IN (
SELECT DISTINCT commerIcial_project_id_new FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0 WHERE prd_filter_group_flag = 1);

END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE     PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_PRC]
AS
BEGIN

BEGIN
DECLARE
@p1 VARCHAR(100),@p2 VARCHAR(100),@p3 VARCHAR(100),@p4 VARCHAR(100),@p5 VARCHAR(100),@p6 VARCHAR(100),
@p7 VARCHAR(100),@p8 VARCHAR(100),@p9 VARCHAR(100),@p10 VARCHAR(100),@p11 VARCHAR(100),@p12 VARCHAR(100),@p13 VARCHAR(100);


DECLARE VP_CURSOR CURSOR FOR 
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_V;

TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG];

OPEN VP_CURSOR;

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13;

WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN

	IF @P12 IN ('One Off')
	BEGIN
	      INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
		  SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',@P6,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13;
	END

   ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Annually')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',START_DT,@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END 
	ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Quarterly')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END

   ELSE --Monthly and others
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);

	END

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13;

END

CLOSE VP_CURSOR;
DEALLOCATE VP_CURSOR;

END;

BEGIN

INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
SELECT 
commercial_project_id, --1,
item_number_of_the_SD_document,--2
'1' dummy_seq, --3,
CASE WHEN new_frequency IN ('One Time','Annual') THEN billing_date_vf
     ELSE END_DATE_WP_ETL
	 END dummy_billing_date, --4,
STR(CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1
     WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN
            CASE WHEN new_frequency IN ('Tri-Annually') THEN 
			                                            CASE WHEN P.CURRENCY_P IS NOT NULL THEN ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/4,0) 
														ELSE ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/4,2)
														END 
	             WHEN new_frequency IN ('Half Yearly') THEN 
			                                            CASE WHEN P.CURRENCY_P IS NOT NULL THEN ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/6,0) 
														ELSE ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/6,2)
														END 				 
	            ELSE 
				                                        CASE WHEN P.CURRENCY_P IS NOT NULL THEN ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT),0) 
														ELSE CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)
														END 
				END
END,30,2) AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,--5
billing_date_vf Service_Start_Date_ETL,--6
--DATEADD(YEAR,1,CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE)) Service_Start_Date_ETL,
END_DATE_WP_ETL Service_End_Date_ETL,--7
material_number,--8
wp_description,--9
Sales_Document_Item_Category AS sales_document_item_category,--10
src,--11,
CASE WHEN new_frequency = 'One Time' THEN 'One Off' 
     WHEN new_frequency = 'Annual' THEN 'Annually' 
     WHEN new_frequency = 'Quarterly' THEN 'Quarterly' 
	 WHEN new_frequency IS NULL OR new_frequency='NULL' THEN 'Annually'
	 ELSE new_frequency
	 END AS frequency , --12
profit_center_item --13
--start_date_wp_etl,fromdate,todate,charge_per,total_fee
FROM 
dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL WP
LEFT OUTER JOIN SAP_IN_PROJECT_CURRENCY_PRECISION P
ON WP.CURRENCY = P.CURRENCY_P
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
SELECT 1 
FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG B
WHERE  WP.commercial_project_id = B.commercial_project_id AND
       WP.item_number_of_the_SD_document = B.item_number_of_the_SD_document
	   );

END;

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_PRC_BEFORE_MAJOR_CHANGE]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE                 PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_PRC_BEFORE_MAJOR_CHANGE]
AS
BEGIN

BEGIN
DECLARE
@p1 VARCHAR(100),@p2 VARCHAR(100),@p3 VARCHAR(100),@p4 VARCHAR(100),@p5 VARCHAR(100),@p6 VARCHAR(100),
@p7 VARCHAR(100),@p8 VARCHAR(100),@p9 VARCHAR(100),@p10 VARCHAR(100),@p11 VARCHAR(100),@p12 VARCHAR(100),@p13 VARCHAR(100);


DECLARE VP_CURSOR CURSOR FOR 
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_V;

TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG];

OPEN VP_CURSOR;

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13;

WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
BEGIN

	IF @P12 IN ('One Off')
	BEGIN
	      INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
		  SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',@P6,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13;
	END

   ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Annually')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',START_DT,@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(YEAR, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END 
	ELSE IF @P12 IN ('Quarterly')
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(QUARTER, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);
	END

   ELSE --Monthly and others
	BEGIN
     WITH DateList AS (
       SELECT CAST(@P6 AS DATE) AS START_DT
       UNION ALL
       SELECT DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)
       FROM DateList
       WHERE CAST(START_DT AS DATE) < CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
     )
     INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
	 SELECT @P1,@P2,'1',DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P5,START_DT,DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)),@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13
     FROM DateList
	 WHERE DATEADD(DAY,-1,DATEADD(MONTH, 1, START_DT)) <= CAST(@P7 AS DATE)
    OPTION (MAXRECURSION 0);

	END

FETCH NEXT FROM VP_CURSOR INTO @P1,@P2,@P3,@P4,@P5,@P6,@P7,@P8,@P9,@P10,@P11,@P12,@P13;

END

CLOSE VP_CURSOR;
DEALLOCATE VP_CURSOR;

END;

BEGIN

INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG
SELECT 
commercial_project_id, --1,
item_number_of_the_SD_document,--2
'1' dummy_seq, --3,
CASE WHEN new_frequency IN ('One Time','Annual') THEN billing_date_vf
     ELSE END_DATE_WP_ETL
	 END dummy_billing_date, --4,
STR(CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1
     WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN
            CASE WHEN new_frequency IN ('Tri-Annually') THEN 
			                                            CASE WHEN P.CURRENCY_P IS NOT NULL THEN ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/4,0) 
														ELSE ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/4,2)
														END 
	             WHEN new_frequency IN ('Half Yearly') THEN 
			                                            CASE WHEN P.CURRENCY_P IS NOT NULL THEN ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/6,0) 
														ELSE ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)/6,2)
														END 				 
	            ELSE 
				                                        CASE WHEN P.CURRENCY_P IS NOT NULL THEN ROUND(CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT),0) 
														ELSE CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT)
														END 
				END
END,30,2) AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,--5
billing_date_vf Service_Start_Date_ETL,--6
--DATEADD(YEAR,1,CAST(SUBSTRING(CASE WHEN SRC = 'DRE' THEN start_date_wp_etl ELSE fromdate END,1,10) AS DATE)) Service_Start_Date_ETL,
END_DATE_WP_ETL Service_End_Date_ETL,--7
material_number,--8
wp_description,--9
Sales_Document_Item_Category AS sales_document_item_category,--10
src,--11,
CASE WHEN new_frequency = 'One Time' THEN 'One Off' 
     WHEN new_frequency = 'Annual' THEN 'Annually' 
     WHEN new_frequency = 'Quarterly' THEN 'Quarterly' 
	 WHEN new_frequency IS NULL OR new_frequency='NULL' THEN 'Annually'
	 ELSE new_frequency
	 END AS frequency , --12
profit_center_item --13
--start_date_wp_etl,fromdate,todate,charge_per,total_fee
FROM 
dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL WP
LEFT OUTER JOIN SAP_IN_PROJECT_CURRENCY_PRECISION P
ON WP.CURRENCY = P.CURRENCY_P
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
SELECT 1 
FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BILLING_STG B
WHERE  WP.commercial_project_id = B.commercial_project_id AND
       WP.item_number_of_the_SD_document = B.item_number_of_the_SD_document
	   );

END;

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BKP]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE               PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BKP] 
AS
BEGIN

EXEC [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY_PRC];

TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2;
--TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER;

WITH WP AS
(
SELECT 
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old 
                        ORDER BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,bill_to_key,currency_key,Execution_Country_key,category_key
          			    )  AS VARCHAR(100))  new_project_number,
w.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       wp.[Project_Definition]  AS Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       wp.Work_Package_WBS, 
	   wp.[Work_Package_WBS_Desc],
	   COALESCE(bill_to,'0') AS bill_to_key,
	   COALESCE(currency,'0') AS currency_key,
       CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL THEN 'G1' 
	        WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NOT NULL THEN wp.Execution_Country
			WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NULL THEN LEFT(wp.Company_Code,2) 
			END AS Execution_Country_Key,
	   COALESCE(a.category,'0') category_key,
	   UPPER(COALESCE(product, '0')) as product_key, 
	   CASE WHEN a.product_advisory IS NOT NULL THEN '1' ELSE '0' END AS advisory_flag_key,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='LEGAL' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END legal_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='TAX'   THEN '1' ELSE 0 END tax_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='HR'    THEN '1' ELSE 0 END hr_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN CHARINDEX('DRE', UPPER(COALESCE(product_1, '0')))>0 THEN '1' ELSE 0 END dre_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN b.action = 'FILTER' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END prd_filter_flag
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
INNER JOIN
(
   SELECT *--P1.Project-- , p1.Project_Name,p1.end_date
   FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P1
   WHERE P1.Current_Stage NOT IN ('Closed','Completed') AND
         (UPPER(P1.Company_code)  NOT LIKE '%CN07%' AND UPPER(P1.Company_code)   NOT LIKE 'ZZ%') AND
		 P1.Project  IN (SELECT project_name FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER] WHERE comment = 'Y') AND
		 UPPER(p1.Project_Name) NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND UPPER(TRIM(p1.Project_Name)) NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND UPPER(REPLACE(p1.Project_Name,' ','')) NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND
		 CAST(p1.End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) 
) P1
ON wp.Project_Definition = P1.project
INNER JOIN SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY F
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = f.plan_item_vf AND
   wp.[Project_Definition] = f.[Project_Definition_vf]
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_ADVISORY A
ON wp.PRODUCT = A.PRODUCT_ADVISORY
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.sap_in_project_product_bridge b
ON wp.PRODUCT = B.PRODUCT_OLD
WHERE 
wp.Stage NOT IN ('P004','P005') AND  
wp.Product IS NOT NULL AND
--wp.PRODUCT NOT IN (SELECT PRODUCT FROM DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_REMOVE ) AND
CAST(wp.Work_Package_End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) AND
UPPER(Work_Package_Name) NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND UPPER(REPLACE(WORK_PACKAGE_NAME,' ','')) NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%'
) w
),
WP1 AS
(
SELECT 'M2'+Commericial_Project_id_Old+'A'+new_project_number AS Commericial_Project_id_new, WP.*,
MAX(dre_exists_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS dre_exists_group_flag,
MAX(prd_filter_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS prd_filter_group_flag
FROM WP 
),
WP2 AS
(--Everything
SELECT * FROM WP1 --WHERE prd_filter_group_flag <> 1
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
SELECT * FROM WP2;

WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
SELECT * FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY 
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);


WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
), 
WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,'ORIGINAL' SRC 
FROM
WP2 x WHERE x.Work_Package_WBS NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT y.Work_Package_WBS 
                                        FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY y
										WHERE y.src NOT LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
									  )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
SELECT * FROM WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);


WITH ALL_DATA AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
UNION 
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER 
SELECT z.*,CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_old ORDER BY work_package_wbs)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_etl_join,
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_new ORDER BY work_package_wbs,src)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_group_etl_join,
CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), GETDATE(), 120) AS ENTRY_DATE,
'Y' Active_flag
FROM ALL_DATA z
WHERE Z.Commericial_Project_id_Old NOT IN (SELECT i.Commericial_Project_id_Old FROM dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER i)
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

UPDATE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER 
SET ACTIVE_FLAG = 'N - FILTER'
WHERE commericial_project_id_new IN (
SELECT DISTINCT commerIcial_project_id_new FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0 WHERE prd_filter_group_flag = 1);

END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BKP_ML2.1_BEFORE]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE       PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BKP_ML2.1_BEFORE] 
AS
BEGIN


EXEC [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC];
PRINT 'Complete Freq_prc';

TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1;
TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2;
--TRUNCATE TABLE  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER;

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0';
WITH WP AS
(
SELECT 
CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old 
                        ORDER BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,bill_to_key,currency_key,Execution_Country_key,category_key
          			    )  AS VARCHAR(100))  new_project_number,
w.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       wp.[Project_Definition]  AS Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       wp.Work_Package_WBS, 
	   wp.[Work_Package_WBS_Desc],
	   COALESCE(bill_to,'0') AS bill_to_key,
	   COALESCE(currency,'0') AS currency_key,
       CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL THEN 'G1' 
	        WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NOT NULL THEN wp.Execution_Country
			WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NULL THEN LEFT(wp.Company_Code,2) 
			END AS Execution_Country_Key,
	   COALESCE(a.category,'0') category_key,
	   UPPER(COALESCE(product, '0')) as product_key, 
	   CASE WHEN a.product_advisory IS NOT NULL THEN '1' ELSE '0' END AS advisory_flag_key,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='LEGAL' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END legal_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='TAX'   THEN '1' ELSE 0 END tax_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL AND UPPER(a.category)='HR'    THEN '1' ELSE 0 END hr_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN CHARINDEX('DRE', UPPER(COALESCE(product_1, '0')))>0 THEN '1' ELSE 0 END dre_exists_flag,
	   CASE WHEN b.action = 'FILTER' THEN '1' ELSE 0 END prd_filter_flag
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
INNER JOIN SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ F
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = f.plan_item_vf AND
   wp.[Project_Definition] = f.[Project_Definition_vf]
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_ADVISORY A
ON wp.PRODUCT = A.PRODUCT_ADVISORY
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.sap_in_project_product_bridge b
ON wp.PRODUCT = B.PRODUCT_OLD
) w
),
WP1 AS
(
SELECT 'M2'+Commericial_Project_id_Old+'A'+new_project_number AS Commericial_Project_id_new, WP.*,
MAX(dre_exists_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS dre_exists_group_flag,
MAX(prd_filter_flag) OVER (PARTITION BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,new_project_number) AS prd_filter_group_flag
FROM WP 
),
WP2 AS
(--Everything
SELECT * FROM WP1 --WHERE prd_filter_group_flag <> 1
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
SELECT * FROM WP2;

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1';
WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
SELECT * FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY 
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2';
WITH WP2 AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0
),
WP3_LEGAL AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_LEGAL' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and legal_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_TAX AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_TAX' SRC) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and tax_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_HR AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR1' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_HR2' ) clone
WHERE advisory_flag_key=1 and hr_exists_flag = 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_DRE AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,MAX(work_package_wbs) work_package_wbs,clone.src
FROM WP2
CROSS JOIN 
(SELECT 'ORIGINAL' SRC UNION ALL SELECT 'CLONE_DRE' SRC) clone
WHERE dre_exists_group_flag <> 1 
GROUP BY Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new, clone.src
),
WP3_BUDDY AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,x2.SRC 
FROM WP2 x1
INNER JOIN
SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY x2 ON
x1.product_key = x2.JOIN_KEY
),
WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY AS
(
SELECT * FROM WP3_LEGAL
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_TAX
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_HR
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_DRE
UNION 
SELECT * FROM WP3_BUDDY WHERE work_package_wbs IN (SELECT MAX(b.work_package_wbs)
                               FROM WP3_BUDDY b
							   WHERE b.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
							   GROUP BY b.Commericial_Project_id_new,b.SRC
							   )
), 
WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT AS
(
SELECT Commericial_Project_id_Old,Commericial_Project_id_new,work_package_wbs,'ORIGINAL' SRC 
FROM
WP2 x WHERE x.Work_Package_WBS NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT y.Work_Package_WBS 
                                        FROM WP3_DEFAULT_ONLY y
										WHERE y.src NOT LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%'
									  )
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
SELECT * FROM WP3_WITHOUT_DEFAULT OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER';
WITH ALL_DATA AS
(
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP1
UNION 
SELECT * FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP2
) 
INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER

CAST(DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY commericial_project_id_new ORDER BY work_package_wbs,src)  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS sequence_number_group_etl_join,
CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), GETDATE(), 120) AS ENTRY_DATE,
'Y' Active_flag
FROM ALL_DATA z
WHERE Z.Commericial_Project_id_Old NOT IN (SELECT i.Commericial_Project_id_Old FROM dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER i)
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'UPDATE PROJECT FILTER';
UPDATE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER 
SET ACTIVE_FLAG = 'N - FILTER'
WHERE commericial_project_id_new IN (
SELECT DISTINCT commerIcial_project_id_new FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_TMP0 WHERE prd_filter_group_flag = 1);
