/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE             PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC] AS
BEGIN

PRINT 'Project Filter';
--Place holder to manage batch, comment the below section when running as batch
TRUNCATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER];
INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER]
SELECT DISTINCT project,'Y' FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] ;
--WHERE [Company_code] LIKE 'US%' OR [Company_code] LIKE 'IE%';

PRINT 'Project Truncate Frequency';
TRUNCATE TABLE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ;
--DROP TABLE IF EXISTS SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ;


PRINT 'Project Frequency';
WITH VF0 AS
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       w.Project_Definition AS Project_Definition_vf, 
       w.work_package_wbs AS plan_item_vf, 
	   w.work_package_wbs_desc  work_package_wbs_desc_vf,
	   p1.sold as sold_vf,
	   p1.Company_code AS company_code_vf,
	   w.[Product] product_vf,
	   w.New_Billing_Amount AS NET_VALUE_vf_original,
	   w.New_Billing_Amount AS NET_VALUE_vf,
       w.New_Service_Start_Date AS settlement_start_date_vf, 
       w.New_Service_end_Date AS settlement_end_date_vf,
       CAST(SUBSTRING(w.New_Billing_Date,1,10) AS DATE) AS billing_date_vf,
	   CAST('N' AS VARCHAR(100)) AS admin_fee_flag,
	   w.New_Item_Category,
	   w.Frequency,
	   w.New_Product,
	   w.New_Product_Group
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] w
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P1
ON w.Project_Definition = P1.project 
AND P1.Project  IN (SELECT project_name FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER] WHERE comment = 'Y')
)
INSERT INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ
SELECT DISTINCT * --INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ 
FROM VF0
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10); 

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - WBS';
--ADMIN FEE
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-WORKPACKAGE',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 and wbs <> ''
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.plan_item_vf = af.wbs AND
(F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'US%' OR F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'IE%'); 

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - PROJECT';
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-PROJECT',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.Project_Definition_vf = af.project AND
(F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'US%' OR F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'IE%');


PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - CUSTOMER';
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-CUSTOMER',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.sold_vf = af.customer AND
(F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'US%' OR F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'IE%');

END;


GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC_before_major_change]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE           PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC_before_major_change] AS
BEGIN

PRINT 'Project Filter';
--Place holder to manage batch, comment the below section when running as batch
TRUNCATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER];
INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER]
SELECT DISTINCT project,'Y' FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] ;
--WHERE [Company_code] LIKE 'US%' OR [Company_code] LIKE 'IE%';

PRINT 'Project Truncate Frequency';
TRUNCATE TABLE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ;
--DROP TABLE IF EXISTS SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ;

--PRINT 'Project DRE Update';
--data quality issue fix
--UPDATE WP
--SET product = 'DISB0001PTE', 
--Item_Category='PS02' 
--from [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
--where wp.[Product]='DV0001PTE';

PRINT 'Project Frequency';
WITH VF0 AS
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       v.Project_Definition AS Project_Definition_vf, 
       v.plan_item AS plan_item_vf, 
	   w.work_package_wbs_desc  work_package_wbs_desc_vf,
	   p1.sold as sold_vf,
	   p1.Company_code AS company_code_vf,
	   w.[Product] product_vf,
	   v.NET_VALUE AS NET_VALUE_vf_original,
	   v.NET_VALUE AS NET_VALUE_vf,
       v.settlement_start_date AS settlement_start_date_vf, 
       v.settlement_end_date AS settlement_end_date_vf,
       CAST(SUBSTRING(v.billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) AS billing_date_vf,
       DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY v.Project_Definition, v.plan_item ORDER BY CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) DESC) RNK_vf,
	   --DATEDIFF(day, settlement_start_date,settlement_end_date) DAYS_DIFF_SETTLEMENT_DATE_vf,
	   CAST('N' AS VARCHAR(100)) AS admin_fee_flag,
	   prd.New_Item_Category,
	   prd.New_Frequency,
	   prd.New_Product,
	   prd.New_Product_Group
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE_CUSTOMER] v
INNER JOIN 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] w
ON w.Work_Package_WBS = v.Plan_Item AND
w.Stage IN ('P003') AND  
CAST(w.Work_Package_End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) AND
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%SETUP%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%ONETIME%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%ONBOARDING%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%DEPOSIT%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%OFFBOARDING%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%OUTOFSCOPE%' AND
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND
w.Currency IS NOT NULL AND
UPPER(w.PRODUCT) NOT LIKE '%CU%' AND 
UPPER(w.PRODUCT) NOT LIKE '%DEP%' AND
CAST(SUBSTRING(v.billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) >= CAST('2024-01-01' AS DATE) AND 
CAST(SUBSTRING(v.billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) <= CAST('2029-12-31' AS DATE) AND
v.Processing_Status IN ('Rejected','Invoiced') 
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P1
ON w.Project_Definition = P1.project AND
P1.Current_Stage IN ('In Execution') AND
(UPPER(P1.Company_code)  NOT LIKE '%CN07%' AND UPPER(P1.Company_code)   NOT LIKE 'ZZ%') AND
P1.Project  IN (SELECT project_name FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER] WHERE comment = 'Y') AND
REPLACE(UPPER(p1.Project_Name),' ','') NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(p1.Project_Name),' ','') NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND
CAST(p1.End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) 
INNER JOIN [SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_MAPPING] PRD
ON PRD.Legacy_Product = W.PRODUCT
),
VF AS
(
SELECT VF0.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY  Project_Definition_vf,plan_item_vf,rnk_vf ORDER BY rnk_vf) ROW_NUM_vf
FROM VF0
),
MAX1 AS
(
SELECT *
FROM VF
WHERE rnk_vf = 1 AND row_num_vf = 1
)
/*,
MAX2 AS
(
SELECT *
FROM VF
WHERE rnk_vf = 2 AND row_num_vf = 1
),
FREQUENCY AS
(
SELECT max1.*,
MAX2.billing_date_vf billing_date_2_vf, 
DATEDIFF(day, MAX2.billing_date_vf,MAX1.billing_date_vf) DAYS_DIFF_vf
FROM MAX1
LEFT OUTER JOIN MAX2
ON MAX1.Project_Definition_vf = MAX2.Project_Definition_vf AND MAX1.plan_item_vf=MAX2.plan_item_vf
),
FINAL_FREQUENCY AS
(
SELECT F.*, 
CASE WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf >= 326 OR billing_date_2_vf IS NULL THEN 'Annually'
     WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf >= 81 AND DAYS_DIFF_vf <= 325 THEN 'Quarterly' 
     WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf <= 80 THEN 'Monthly' 

END Frequency 
FROM FREQUENCY F 
) */
INSERT INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ
SELECT DISTINCT * --INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ 
FROM MAX1
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10); --WHERE billing_date_2_vf IS NOT NULL

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - WBS';
--ADMIN FEE
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-WORKPACKAGE',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 and wbs <> ''
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.plan_item_vf = af.wbs AND
(F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'US%' OR F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'IE%'); 

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - PROJECT';
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-PROJECT',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.Project_Definition_vf = af.project AND
(F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'US%' OR F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'IE%');


PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - CUSTOMER';
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-CUSTOMER',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.sold_vf = af.customer AND
(F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'US%' OR F.[Company_code_vf] LIKE 'IE%');

END;

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC_BKP]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE                     PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ_PRC_BKP] AS
BEGIN

PRINT 'Project Filter';
--Place holder to manage batch, comment the below section when running as batch
TRUNCATE TABLE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER];
INSERT INTO [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER]
SELECT DISTINCT project,'Y' FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] ;
--WHERE [Company_code] LIKE 'US%' OR [Company_code] LIKE 'IE%';

PRINT 'Project Truncate Frequency';
TRUNCATE TABLE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ;
--DROP TABLE IF EXISTS SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ;

PRINT 'Project DRE Update';
--data quality issue fix
UPDATE WP
SET product = 'DISB0001PTE', 
Item_Category='PS02' 
from [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
where wp.[Product]='DV0001PTE';

PRINT 'Project Frequency';
WITH VF0 AS
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       v.Project_Definition AS Project_Definition_vf, 
       v.plan_item AS plan_item_vf, 
	   w.work_package_wbs_desc  work_package_wbs_desc_vf,
	   p1.sold as sold_vf,
	   p1.Company_code AS company_code_vf,
	   w.[Product] product_vf,
	   v.NET_VALUE AS NET_VALUE_vf_original,
	   v.NET_VALUE AS NET_VALUE_vf,
       v.settlement_start_date AS settlement_start_date_vf, 
       v.settlement_end_date AS settlement_end_date_vf,
       CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) AS billing_date_vf,
       DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY v.Project_Definition, v.plan_item ORDER BY CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) DESC) RNK_vf,
	   DATEDIFF(day, settlement_start_date,settlement_end_date) DAYS_DIFF_SETTLEMENT_DATE_vf,
	   CAST('N' AS VARCHAR(100)) AS admin_fee_flag
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE_CUSTOMER] v
INNER JOIN 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] w
ON w.Work_Package_WBS = v.Plan_Item AND
w.Stage NOT IN ('P004','P005') AND  
w.Product IS NOT NULL AND
CAST(w.Work_Package_End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) AND
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%SETUP%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%ONETIME%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%ONBOARDING%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%DEPOSIT%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%OFFBOARDING%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%OUTOFSCOPE%' AND
REPLACE(UPPER(w.work_package_wbs_desc),' ','') NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND
UPPER(w.PRODUCT) NOT LIKE '%CU%' AND 
UPPER(w.PRODUCT) NOT LIKE '%DEP%' AND
w.Project_Definition IS NOT NULL AND
w.Work_Package_Name  IS NOT NULL AND
CAST(SUBSTRING(v.billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) >= CAST('2024-01-01' AS DATE) AND 
CAST(SUBSTRING(v.billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) <= CAST('2029-12-31' AS DATE) AND
v.Processing_Status IN ('Rejected','Invoiced') 
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P1
ON w.Project_Definition = P1.project AND
P1.Current_Stage NOT IN ('Closed','Completed') AND
(UPPER(P1.Company_code)  NOT LIKE '%CN07%' AND UPPER(P1.Company_code)   NOT LIKE 'ZZ%') AND
P1.Project  IN (SELECT project_name FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_FILTER] WHERE comment = 'Y') AND
REPLACE(UPPER(p1.Project_Name),' ','') NOT LIKE '%CLOSED%' AND 
REPLACE(UPPER(p1.Project_Name),' ','') NOT LIKE '%DONOTUSE%' AND
CAST(p1.End_Date AS DATE) > CAST('2024-12-31' AS DATE) 
),
VF AS
(
SELECT VF0.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY  Project_Definition_vf,plan_item_vf,rnk_vf ORDER BY rnk_vf) ROW_NUM_vf
FROM VF0
),
MAX1 AS
(
SELECT *
FROM VF
WHERE rnk_vf = 1 AND row_num_vf = 1
),
MAX2 AS
(
SELECT *
FROM VF
WHERE rnk_vf = 2 AND row_num_vf = 1
),
FREQUENCY AS
(
SELECT max1.*,
MAX2.billing_date_vf billing_date_2_vf, 
DATEDIFF(day, MAX2.billing_date_vf,MAX1.billing_date_vf) DAYS_DIFF_vf
FROM MAX1
LEFT OUTER JOIN MAX2
ON MAX1.Project_Definition_vf = MAX2.Project_Definition_vf AND MAX1.plan_item_vf=MAX2.plan_item_vf
),
FINAL_FREQUENCY AS
(
SELECT F.*, 
CASE WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf >= 326 OR billing_date_2_vf IS NULL THEN 'Annually'
     WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf >= 81 AND DAYS_DIFF_vf <= 325 THEN 'Quarterly' 
     WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf <= 80 THEN 'Monthly' 

END Frequency 
FROM FREQUENCY F 
) 
INSERT INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ
SELECT DISTINCT * --INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ 
FROM FINAL_FREQUENCY 
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10); --WHERE billing_date_2_vf IS NOT NULL

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - WBS';
--ADMIN FEE
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-WORKPACKAGE',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 and wbs <> ''
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.plan_item_vf = af.wbs; 

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - PROJECT';
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-PROJECT',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.Project_Definition_vf = af.project;

PRINT 'Project ADMIN FEE - CUSTOMER';
UPDATE F
SET admin_fee_flag = 'Y-CUSTOMER',
    f.NET_VALUE_vf = STR(f.NET_VALUE_vf - f.NET_VALUE_vf * af.fee/100,30,2)
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] F
INNER JOIN
(
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_ADMIN_FEE] 
WHERE CAST(FEE AS FLOAT) <> 0 
) AF
ON f.company_code_vf = af.SALES_ORG AND
   f.admin_fee_flag  = 'N' AND
F.sold_vf = af.customer;

END;

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE              PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRC] 
AS
BEGIN

--TRUNCATE TABLE  DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRE;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRE;

--INSERT INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRE
SELECT  
     CASE WHEN Work_Package_Name_COUNT IS NOT NULL AND Work_Package_Name_COUNT <> 1 THEN Work_Package_Name_ETL+'  '+Sequence_Number 
	 ELSE Work_Package_Name_ETL 
	 END AS Work_Package_Name,
	 CASE WHEN segment_name = 'VFS' THEN '50100000'
	      WHEN segment_name = 'VGS' THEN COALESCE(PCTR.PROFIT_center_code,'80100000')
		  ELSE '50100000'
	END AS Profit_Center_item,
     --COALESCE(wp.Profit_Center_wp_etl,Ps.Profit_Center_ps_etl)       AS Profit_Center_etl,
     CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Start_Date_wp_etl AS DATE),104) AS  Start_Date_wp,
	 CDM AS Price_Refresh___Country,
	 CASE WHEN SRC = 'CLONE_TAX' THEN Project_Name_ETL+'_AD_Tax'
	      WHEN SRC = 'CLONE_LEGAL' THEN Project_Name_ETL+'_AD_Legal'
          WHEN SRC LIKE 'CLONE_HR%' THEN Project_Name_ETL+'_AD_HR'
		  ELSE Project_Name_ETL+'_'+CDM
		  END AS Project_Name,
      CASE WHEN WP.Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U' ELSE NULL END AS WP_Type,
      CASE WHEN WP.Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U003' ELSE NULL END AS Service_ID,
      CASE WHEN WP.Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN '1' ELSE NULL END AS Service_Quantity,
	 PS.*,WP.*, WI.*
INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRE
FROM
(
SELECT cctr.Cost_Center_ctr AS Cost_Center,
CCTR.*,
PS.*
FROM 
(
SELECT DISTINCT P.[Project]            AS Commercial_Project_ID_old,
       XREF.CUSTOMER_NEW        AS Customer_ID,
	   'NA' AS Closure_Reason,
	   '01.01.2026' AS First_Price_Refresh_Date,
	   '0' AS PI_______Number,
       'Yes' AS Price_Increase_PI____Indicator,
	   P.[Project_Name]       AS Project_Name_ETL,
	   'SHIKHA.KAKKAR.CONTRACTOR' AS Project_Manager_ID_ETL,
	   '31.12.2040' AS End_Date,
	   P.[Service_Organization] AS Service_Organization,
       P.[Company_code]      AS Company_Code,
	   CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN 'VFS'
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN 'VGS'
			ELSE 'OTHERS'
			END segment_name_original,
	   CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN 'VFS'
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN 'VGS'
			ELSE 'VFS'
			END segment_name,
       CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN '50100000' 
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN '80100000'  
			ELSE '50100000' 
	   END AS Profit_Center,
	   P.[Original_Opportunity_ID] AS Original_Opportunity_ID,
	   P.[Use_Summarised_Invoice_Form] AS [Use_Summarised_Invoice_Form],
	   CASE WHEN P.Current_Stage='In Planning' THEN 'P001'
	        WHEN P.Current_Stage='Contract Preparation' THEN 'P002'
			WHEN P.Current_Stage='In Execution' THEN 'P003'
			WHEN P.Current_Stage='Completed' THEN 'P004'
			WHEN P.Current_Stage='Closed' THEN 'P005'
	   END Stage,
	   'N'                 AS Indicator__Restr__Time_Post__W_O_Staff_,
       'X'                 AS Project_Invoicing_Solution,
	   'C'                  AS Project_Type,
	   REPLACE(C.Project_Controller_ID,'CB','') Project_Controller_Internal_ID_ETL,
       CASE WHEN c.Project_Controller_Role_ID='P003' THEN '0SAP_RL_005' ELSE c.Project_Controller_Role_ID END AS Project_Role_ID,
	   Current_Stage
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P
LEFT OUTER JOIN  [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_CONTROLLER_REPORT] C
ON P.[Project]=C.[customer_project_id]
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF XREF
ON XREF.CUSTOMER_OLD = P.[Sold]
LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_SEGMENT] CTR
ON CTR.Company_Code = P.Company_code AND
CTR.Customer = P.Sold
) PS
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_COST_CTR cctr
ON CHARINDEX(ps.segment_name, cctr.segment_ctr) > 0 AND
   CHARINDEX(ps.Company_Code, cctr.Company_Code_ctr) > 0
) PS
INNER JOIN 
(
SELECT 
 COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY a.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,UPPER(a.Work_Package_Name_ETL)) AS Work_Package_Name_COUNT,
 CONVERT(VARCHAR,MIN(CAST(Start_Date_wp_etl AS DATE)) OVER (PARTITION BY a.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE),104) AS Start_Date,
 CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS01','PS06') 
                           THEN CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT) 
						   ELSE 0 END) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID_PRE),2))  ACV_Value,
A.* 
FROM 
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       d.Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       d.Commericial_Project_id_new AS Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,
	   d.src,
	   f.NET_VALUE_vf,
	   f.NET_VALUE_vf_original,
	   f.admin_fee_flag,
	   wp.New_Billing_Date,
	   wp.New_Service_Start_Date,
	   wp.New_Service_End_Date,
	   wp.Frequency,
       CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL THEN 'G1' 
	        WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NOT NULL THEN wp.Execution_Country
			WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NULL THEN LEFT(Company_Code,2) 
			END AS CDM,
	   wp.Currency AS Currency,
	   d.sequence_number_group_etl_join AS Sequence_Number,
	   d.sequence_number_group_etl_join  AS Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document,
	   wp.Work_Package_WBS, 
       LEFT(TRIM(CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN  wp.[New_Work_Package_Name] ELSE df.Work_Package_Name END),60)  AS Work_Package_Name_ETL,
	   COALESCE(wp.Execution_Country,LEFT(Company_Code,2))+'-'+
	   CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN wp.[New_Work_Package_Description] ELSE df.Work_Package_Name 
	   END  AS  WP_Description,
	   wp.New_Service_Start_Date AS  Start_Date_wp_etl,
	   wp.New_Service_Start_Date AS [Work_Package_Start_Date],
	   '31.12.2030' AS end_date_wp,
	   '2030-12-31' AS end_date_wp_etl,
	   'M2'+CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN wp.NEW_Product
				 ELSE df.Material_Number END  AS Material_Number,
	   CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN wp.NEW_Item_Category
				 ELSE df.Sales_Document_Item_Category END  AS Sales_Document_Item_Category,
	   CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN COALESCE(b.product_description,wp.[New_Work_Package_Name])
				 ELSE df.Work_Package_Name END  AS Material_Description,
	   CASE WHEN wp.[OPP_id] IS NULL OR LEN(wp.OPP_ID)=0 THEN 'CPVT' ELSE wp.OPP_ID END   AS Opportunity_ID,
	   --NULL AS Opportunity_ID,
       SUBSTRING(wp.New_Service_Start_Date,1,4)  AS Calendar_Year,
	   SUBSTRING(wp.New_Service_Start_Date,6,2) AS Calendar_Month,
	   'S001'                                             AS Work_Package_Function_ID,
     b.action
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER] d
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = d.Work_Package_WBS AND d.ACTIVE_FLAG = 'Y'
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] f
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = f.Plan_Item_vf 
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.sap_in_project_product_bridge b
ON wp.PRODUCT = B.PRODUCT_OLD AND b.action = 'TRANSFORM'
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY df
ON df.src = d.src 
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_ADVISORY A
ON PRODUCT = A.PRODUCT_ADVISORY
) A
) WP
ON PS.Commercial_Project_ID_old = WP.Commericial_Project_id_Old
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
(
SELECT DISTINCT PLAN_ITEM, 
WI.Work_Item_ID,
WI.Work_Item_Name,
WI.Is_Inactive
 FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_project_WorkItem] WI 
 WHERE Work_Item_ID IS NOT NULL AND  1=2
 ) WI
 ON WI.PLAN_ITEM = wp.Work_Package_WBS
 LEFT OUTER JOIN  SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROFIT_CTR_ITEM_V PCTR
 ON 'M2'+PCTR.LEGACY_PRODUCT = WP.Material_Number
WHERE segment_name <> 'OTHERS' AND Customer_ID IS NOT NULL
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

PRINT 'XREF FOR COMMERICAL PROJECT ID';
INSERT INTO Commercial_Project_ID_XREF
SELECT f.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE,
'C'+CAST(NEXT VALUE FOR Commercial_Project_ID_Seq AS NVARCHAR(1000)) AS Commercial_Project_ID,
'SAP' AS SRC
FROM
(SELECT DISTINCT Commercial_Project_ID_PRE FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRE) f
LEFT OUTER JOIN Commercial_Project_ID_XREF xref
ON xref.Commercial_Project_ID_Pre = f.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE
WHERE xref.Commercial_Project_ID IS NULL;

PRINT 'INSERT SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL';
--TRUNCATE TABLE  DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL;

--INSERT INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL
SELECT 
XREF.Commercial_Project_ID AS Commercial_Project_ID,
XREF.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE AS Commercial_Project_ID_PRE_XREF,
F.*
INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL
FROM SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRE F
LEFT OUTER JOIN Commercial_Project_ID_XREF XREF
ON F.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE = XREF.Commercial_Project_ID_PRE;

END;

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRC_BEFORE_ML2.1]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE              PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL_PRC_BEFORE_ML2.1] 
AS
BEGIN

TRUNCATE TABLE  DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL;
--DROP TABLE DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL;

--INSERT INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL
SELECT  
     CASE WHEN Work_Package_Name_COUNT IS NOT NULL AND Work_Package_Name_COUNT <> 1 THEN Work_Package_Name_ETL+'  '+Sequence_Number 
	 ELSE Work_Package_Name_ETL 
	 END AS Work_Package_Name,
	 CASE WHEN segment_name = 'VFS' THEN ps.Profit_Center
	      WHEN segment_name = 'VGS' THEN PCTR.PROFIT_CTR 
		  ELSE NULL
	END AS Profit_Center_item,
     --COALESCE(wp.Profit_Center_wp_etl,Ps.Profit_Center_ps_etl)       AS Profit_Center_etl,
     CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Start_Date_wp_etl AS DATE),104) AS  Start_Date_wp,
	 CDM AS Price_Refresh___Country,
	 CASE WHEN SRC = 'CLONE_TAX' THEN Project_Name_ETL+'_AD_Tax'
	      WHEN SRC = 'CLONE_LEGAL' THEN Project_Name_ETL+'_AD_Legal'
          WHEN SRC LIKE 'CLONE_HR%' THEN Project_Name_ETL+'_AD_HR'
		  ELSE Project_Name_ETL+'_'+CDM
		  END AS Project_Name,
      CASE WHEN WP.Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U' ELSE NULL END AS WP_Type,
      CASE WHEN WP.Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN 'U003' ELSE NULL END AS Service_ID,
      CASE WHEN WP.Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS07') THEN '1' ELSE NULL END AS Service_Quantity,
	 PS.*,WP.*, WI.*
--INTO DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL
FROM
(
SELECT cctr.Cost_Center_ctr AS Cost_Center,
CCTR.*,
PS.*
FROM 
(
SELECT DISTINCT P.[Project]            AS Commercial_Project_ID_old,
       XREF.CUSTOMER_NEW        AS Customer_ID,
	   'NA' AS Closure_Reason,
	   '01.01.2026' AS First_Price_Refresh_Date,
	   '0' AS PI_______Number,
       'Yes' AS Price_Increase_PI____Indicator,
       --P.[Sold]               AS Customer_ID,
	   P.[Project_Name]       AS Project_Name_ETL,
       --REPLACE(P.[Project_Manager_ID],'.0','') AS Project_Manager_ID_ETL,
	   'SHIKHA.KAKKAR.CONTRACTOR' AS Project_Manager_ID_ETL,
       --CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(P.[Start_Date] AS DATE),104)  AS Start_Date,
	   '31.12.2040' AS End_Date,
	   --P.[Project_Currency]   AS Currency,
	   P.[Service_Organization] AS Service_Organization,
       P.[Company_code]      AS Company_Code,
	   CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN 'VFS'
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN 'VGS'
			ELSE 'OTHERS'
			END segment_name,
       CASE WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VFS%' THEN '50100000' 
	        WHEN UPPER(CTR.Segment_Name) LIKE '%VGS%' THEN '80100000'  
			ELSE NULL
	   END AS Profit_Center,
  	   --P.[Profit_Center]     AS Profit_Center_ps_etl,
	   --p.Cost_Center AS Cost_center_etl,
	   P.[Original_Opportunity_ID] AS Original_Opportunity_ID,
	   P.[Use_Summarised_Invoice_Form] AS [Use_Summarised_Invoice_Form],
	   CASE WHEN P.Current_Stage='In Planning' THEN 'P001'
	        WHEN P.Current_Stage='Contract Preparation' THEN 'P002'
			WHEN P.Current_Stage='In Execution' THEN 'P003'
			WHEN P.Current_Stage='Completed' THEN 'P004'
			WHEN P.Current_Stage='Closed' THEN 'P005'
	   END Stage,
	   'N'                 AS Indicator__Restr__Time_Post__W_O_Staff_,
       'X'                 AS Project_Invoicing_Solution,
	   'C'                  AS Project_Type,
	   REPLACE(C.Project_Controller_ID,'CB','') Project_Controller_Internal_ID_ETL,
	  -- 'UTKARSH.SAXENA.CTR' AS Project_Controller_Internal_ID_ETL,
       CASE WHEN c.Project_Controller_Role_ID='P003' THEN '0SAP_RL_005' ELSE c.Project_Controller_Role_ID END AS Project_Role_ID,
--       c.Project_Controller_ID          AS Business_Partner_Number,
	   Current_Stage
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_PROF_SERVICES] P
LEFT OUTER JOIN  [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_CONTROLLER_REPORT] C
ON P.[Project]=C.[customer_project_id]
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_XREF XREF
ON XREF.CUSTOMER_OLD = P.[Sold]
LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_CUSTOMER_SEGMENT] CTR
ON CTR.Company_Code = P.Company_code AND
CTR.Customer = P.Sold
) PS
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_COST_CTR cctr
ON CHARINDEX(ps.segment_name, cctr.segment_ctr) > 0 AND
   CHARINDEX(ps.Company_Code, cctr.Company_Code_ctr) > 0
) PS
INNER JOIN 
(
SELECT 
 COUNT(*) OVER (PARTITION BY a.Commercial_Project_ID,UPPER(a.Work_Package_Name_ETL)) AS Work_Package_Name_COUNT,
 CONVERT(VARCHAR,MIN(Start_Date_wp_etl) OVER (PARTITION BY a.Commercial_Project_ID),104) AS Start_Date,
 CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS01','PS06') 
                           THEN CAST(NET_VALUE_vf AS FLOAT) 
						   ELSE 0 END) OVER (PARTITION BY Commercial_Project_ID),2))  ACV_Value,
A.* 
FROM 
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       d.Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       d.Commericial_Project_id_new AS Commercial_Project_ID,
	   d.src,
       CASE WHEN a.category IS NOT NULL THEN 'G1' 
	        WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NOT NULL THEN wp.Execution_Country
			WHEN a.category IS NULL AND wp.Execution_Country IS NULL THEN LEFT(Company_Code,2) 
			END AS CDM,
	   wp.Currency AS Currency,
	   d.sequence_number_group_etl_join AS Sequence_Number,
	   d.sequence_number_group_etl_join  AS Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document,
	   wp.Work_Package_WBS, 
	   --CASE WHEN LEN(df.Profit_Center)=0 THEN NULL ELSE df.Profit_Center END  AS Profit_Center_wp_etl,
       LEFT(TRIM(CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN  wp.[Work_Package_Name] ELSE df.Work_Package_Name END),60)  AS Work_Package_Name_ETL,
	   --CAST(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY d.Commericial_Project_id_new ORDER BY d.Commericial_Project_id_new) AS VARCHAR(100))     AS Sequence_Number
	   CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' THEN wp.[Work_Package_WBS_Desc] ELSE df.Work_Package_Name END  AS  WP_Description,
	   CASE WHEN CAST(f.billing_date_vf AS DATE) < CAST(wp.[Work_Package_Start_Date] AS DATE) THEN f.billing_date_vf
	        ELSE wp.[Work_Package_Start_Date]
	   END AS  Start_Date_wp_etl,
	   wp.[Work_Package_Start_Date],
       --CONVERT(VARCHAR,CASE WHEN DATEDIFF(YEAR, CAST([Work_Package_Start_Date] AS DATE),CAST([Work_Package_End_Date]  AS DATE) ) > 3 
       --     THEN DATEADD(YEAR, 3, CAST([Work_Package_Start_Date]AS DATE)) 
       --ELSE CAST([Work_Package_End_Date]AS DATE)
	   --END,104)   AS end_date_wp, 	
	   '31.12.2029' AS end_date_wp,
	   '2029-12-31' AS end_date_wp_etl,
	   --CASE WHEN d.src LIKE 'CLONE%' THEN df.WP_Type    ELSE  wp.[Work_package_type] END AS WP_Type,
	   --'U003'       AS Service_ID,
	   --CASE WHEN d.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%' THEN df.Service_Quantity ELSE wp.[Qty]    END        AS Service_Quantity,
	   'M2'+CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' AND b.action='TRANSFORM' THEN b.product_new
				 WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' AND b.action IS NULL THEN wp.[Product]  
				 ELSE df.Material_Number END  AS Material_Number,
	   CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' AND b.action='TRANSFORM' THEN b.item_category
				 WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' AND b.action IS NULL THEN wp.[Item_Category]
				 ELSE df.Sales_Document_Item_Category END  AS Sales_Document_Item_Category,
	   CASE WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' AND b.action='TRANSFORM' THEN b.product_description
				 WHEN d.src = 'ORIGINAL' AND b.action IS NULL THEN wp.[Work_Package_Name]
				 ELSE df.Work_Package_Name END  AS Material_Description,
	   CASE WHEN wp.[OPP_id] IS NULL OR LEN(wp.OPP_ID)=0 THEN 'CPVT' ELSE wp.OPP_ID END   AS Opportunity_ID,
       CASE WHEN d.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%' THEN df.Calendar_Year ELSE SUBSTRING(wp.[Work_Package_Start_Date],1,4) END  AS Calendar_Year,
	   CASE WHEN d.src LIKE 'CLONE_BUDDY%' THEN df.Calendar_Month  ELSE SUBSTRING(wp.[Work_Package_Start_Date],6,2) END  AS Calendar_Month,
	   'S001'                                             AS Work_Package_Function_ID,
     b.action,
	 f.*
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] wp
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_DRIVER] d
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = d.Work_Package_WBS AND d.ACTIVE_FLAG = 'Y'
INNER JOIN [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FILTER_FREQ] f
ON wp.Work_Package_WBS = f.Plan_Item_vf 
LEFT OUTER JOIN dbo.sap_in_project_product_bridge b
ON wp.PRODUCT = B.PRODUCT_OLD AND b.action = 'TRANSFORM'
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_BUDDY df
ON df.src = d.src 
LEFT OUTER JOIN DBO.SAP_IN_PROJECT_PRODUCT_ADVISORY A
ON PRODUCT = A.PRODUCT_ADVISORY
) A
) WP
ON PS.Commercial_Project_ID_old = WP.Commericial_Project_id_Old
LEFT OUTER JOIN 
(
SELECT DISTINCT PLAN_ITEM, 
WI.Work_Item_ID,
WI.Work_Item_Name,
WI.Is_Inactive
 FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_project_WorkItem] WI 
 WHERE Work_Item_ID IS NOT NULL AND  1=2
 ) WI
 ON WI.PLAN_ITEM = wp.Work_Package_WBS
 LEFT OUTER JOIN  dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_PCTR_ITEM PCTR
 ON 'M2'+PCTR.PRODUCT = WP.Material_Number
WHERE customer_id IS NOT NULL AND PCTR.PROFIT_CTR IS NOT NULL AND PS.PROFIT_CENTER IS NOT NULL AND PS.COST_CENTER IS NOT NULL
OPTION (RECOMPILE,FORCE ORDER, MAXDOP 10);

END;
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE        PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY_PRC] AS
BEGIN

--TRUNCATE TABLE SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY;


WITH VF0 AS
(
SELECT DISTINCT v.Project_Definition AS Project_Definition_vf, 
       v.plan_item AS plan_item_vf, 
	   w.work_package_wbs_desc  work_package_wbs_desc_vf,
	   w.[Product],
	   v.NET_VALUE AS NET_VALUE_vf,
       v.settlement_start_date AS settlement_start_date_vf, 
       v.settlement_end_date AS settlement_end_date_vf,
       CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) AS billing_date_vf,
       DENSE_RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY v.Project_Definition, v.plan_item ORDER BY CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) DESC) RNK_vf,
	   DATEDIFF(day, settlement_start_date,settlement_end_date) DAYS_DIFF_SETTLEMENT_DATE_vf
FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE_CUSTOMER] v
INNER JOIN 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WORK_PACKAGE] w
ON w.Work_Package_WBS = v.Plan_Item AND
Processing_Status IN ('Rejected','Invoiced') AND
CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) >= CAST('2024-01-01' AS DATE) AND 
CAST(SUBSTRING(billing_date,1,10) AS DATE) <= CAST('2029-12-31' AS DATE) --AND v.Project_Definition = '1000000019A'
),
VF AS
(
SELECT VF0.*, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY  Project_Definition_vf,plan_item_vf,rnk_vf ORDER BY rnk_vf) ROW_NUM_vf
FROM VF0
),
MAX1 AS
(
SELECT *
FROM VF
WHERE rnk_vf = 1 AND row_num_vf = 1
),
MAX2 AS
(
SELECT *
FROM VF
WHERE rnk_vf = 2 AND row_num_vf = 1
),
FREQUENCY AS
(
SELECT max1.*,
MAX2.billing_date_vf billing_date_2_vf, 
DATEDIFF(day, MAX2.billing_date_vf,MAX1.billing_date_vf) DAYS_DIFF_vf
FROM MAX1
LEFT OUTER JOIN MAX2
ON MAX1.Project_Definition_vf = MAX2.Project_Definition_vf AND MAX1.plan_item_vf=MAX2.plan_item_vf
),
FINAL_FREQUENCY AS
(
SELECT F.*, 
CASE WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf >= 326 OR billing_date_2_vf IS NULL THEN 'Annually'
     WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf >= 81 AND DAYS_DIFF_vf <= 325 THEN 'Quarterly' 
     WHEN DAYS_DIFF_vf <= 80 THEN 'Monthly' 

END Frequency 
FROM FREQUENCY F 
) 
--INSERT INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY
SELECT DISTINCT * INTO SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VF_FREQUENCY 
FROM FINAL_FREQUENCY;

END;

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VFORCE_PRC]    Script Date: 1/15/2026 10:54:34 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE   PROCEDURE [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_VFORCE_PRC]
AS
BEGIN

TRUNCATE TABLE dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE;
--DROP TABLE dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE;

INSERT INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE
SELECT * 
--INTO dbo.SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE
FROM 
(
SELECT DISTINCT
  STR(CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN 1 
	        WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN CAST(NET_VALUE_ETL AS FLOAT)
			ELSE NULL
		END,30,2)  AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency,
  STR(CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS02','PS07') THEN NULL 
	        WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS01','PS06') THEN ABS(CAST(BILLING_VALUE_ETL AS FLOAT))
			ELSE NULL
		END,30,2) AS Net_Value_in_Document_Currency_Billing,
CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category = 'PS06' AND A.Billing_Date_ETL>=A.Service_Start_Date_etl AND A.Billing_Date_ETL<=A.Service_End_Date_etl  AND A.Billing_Date_ETL>=A.start_date_wp  AND A.Billing_Date_ETL<=A.end_date_wp THEN 'YES'  
     WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category <> 'PS06' AND A.Billing_Date_ETL>=A.start_date_wp  AND A.Billing_Date_ETL<=A.end_date_wp THEN 'YES' 
	 ELSE 'NO'     
	 END
     Billing_flag,
CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS06') THEN Service_Start_Date_VF_ETL ELSE NULL END AS Service_Start_Date,
CASE WHEN Sales_Document_Item_Category IN ('PS06') THEN Service_End_Date_VF_ETL  ELSE NULL END  AS Service_End_Date ,
A.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
WP.*, VF.*
FROM
(
SELECT DISTINCT 
       Commericial_Project_id_Old,
       Commercial_Project_ID,
	   Item_Number_of_the_SD_Document,
	   Work_Package_WBS, 
	   src,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Start_Date_wp_etl AS DATE),112) Start_Date_wp,
	   CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(work_package_end_date AS DATE),112) end_date_wp,
	   Sales_Document_Item_Category,
	   Material_Description,
	   Material_number
FROM 
[dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_WP_FINAL] d
) WP
INNER JOIN 
(
SELECT DISTINCT [Project_Definition] AS Commercial_Project_ID_OLD, plan_item,Item_1
	  ,CAST(ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY [Project_Definition],[plan_item] ORDER BY [Billing_Date])  AS VARCHAR(100))   AS Item_for_Billing_Plan_Invoice_Plan_Paym
	  ,NET_VALUE AS NET_VALUE_ETL
	  ,Billing_Value AS Billing_Value_ETL
      ,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Settlement_Start_Date AS DATE),104) AS Service_Start_Date_VF_ETL
      ,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Settlement_End_Date AS DATE),104)   AS Service_End_Date_VF_ETL 
      ,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST([Billing_Date] AS DATE),104) AS Billing_Due_Date
	  ,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Settlement_Start_Date AS DATE),112) AS Service_Start_Date_ETL
	  ,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST(Settlement_End_Date AS DATE),112) AS Service_End_Date_ETL
	  ,CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST([Billing_Date] AS DATE),112) AS Billing_Date_ETL
      ,[profit_center] AS Profit_Center_etl
--      ,[product]   AS Material_Number
--      ,[Item_Description]   AS Material_Description
--      ,[Item_Category]   AS Sales_Document_Item_Category_ETL
--      ,'PBS00001'  AS Dynamic_Item_Processor_Profile
	  ,processing_status
    FROM [dbo].[SAP_IN_PROJECT_VFORCE_CUSTOMER]
	WHERE --CONVERT(VARCHAR,CAST([Billing_Date] AS DATE),112) >= '20250101' AND 
	processing_status IN ('Open','Billing Requested')
) VF
ON WP.Commericial_Project_id_Old = VF.Commercial_Project_ID_OLD AND
wp.Work_Package_WBS = VF.plan_item
)A
 ) B
WHERE BILLING_FLAG = 'YES';

END;
GO
USE [master]
GO
ALTER DATABASE [SAP_DM_DEV] SET  READ_WRITE 
GO
